	depth -= 1;

		<div class="disclaimer__row">
				<sup>ε</sup>Terms and conditions apply.
			</div>
			<div></div>

	</div>
</section>
<script type="text/javascript">
	window.addEventListener('load', function(event){
		if($) {
			var $disclaimer = $('.disclaimer__row');
			var $disclaimer_single = $('.disclaimer__single');

			var init = function() {
			    var disclaimerWidth = $disclaimer[0].offsetWidth,
	                rowWidth = 0;
	            var formatDisclaimer = function ($item, resize) {
	                var resize = resize || false;
	                var strings = $item.text(),
	                    htmlStrings = $item.attr('data-default').length > $item.html().length ? $item.attr('data-default') : $item.html(),
	                    shortString = '',
	                    charsWidth = -1,
	                    stringLength = 0,
	                    limitLength = $disclaimer.width();

	                if (strings.length > 0) {
	                    var temp = $item.html();
	                    $item.text('Abcd efgh ');
	                    charsWidth = $item.width();
	                    rowWidth = rowWidth || $disclaimer.width();
	                    stringLength = Math.floor((limitLength - charsWidth) / charsWidth) * 10 + superscriptLength(htmlStrings);
	                    shortString = htmlStrings.slice(0, stringLength);
	                    var lastSpace = shortString.lastIndexOf(' ');
	                    shortString = shortString.slice(0, lastSpace) + '...';
	                    if(resize) {
	                        $item.attr('data-default', shortString);
	                        $item.html(temp);
	                    }
	                    else
	                        $item.html(shortString);
	                }
	            };

	            var superscriptLength = function (string) {
	                var len = 0,
	                    sup = string.substring(0,50).split("<sup>").length - 1,
	                    b = string.substring(0,50).split("<b>").length - 1;
	                len += sup * 13 + b * 8;
	                return len;
	            };

	            var swapText = function ($item) {
	                var temp = $item.attr('data-default'),
	                    text = $item.html();
	                $item.attr('data-default', text);
	                $item.html(temp);
	            };
			    if($disclaimer_single && $disclaimer_single.length > 0) {
	                _.forEach($disclaimer_single, function (item, idx) {
	                    if(item.offsetWidth <= disclaimerWidth) {
	                        $(item).siblings('.disclaimer__hide__single').hide();
	                        $(item).siblings('.disclaimer__show__single').hide();
	                    }
	                    else {
	                        $(item).siblings('.disclaimer__hide__single').hide();
	                        $(item).siblings('.disclaimer__show__single').show();
	                        formatDisclaimer($(item));
	                    }
	                });
	            }

	            $('.disclaimer__show__link').on('click', function (e) {
	                e.preventDefault();
	                $(this).parent().hide();
	                $(this).parent().siblings('.disclaimer__hide').show();
	            });
	            $('.disclaimer__hide__link').on('click', function (e) {
	                e.preventDefault();
	                $(this).parent().hide();
	                $(this).parent().siblings('.disclaimer__show').show();
	            });
	            $('.disclaimer__show__single').on('click', function (e) {
	                e.preventDefault();
	                var $target = $(this).siblings('.disclaimer__single');
	                swapText($target);
	                $target.css('white-space', 'normal');
	                $(this).hide();
	                $(this).siblings('.disclaimer__hide__single').show();
	            });
	            $('.disclaimer__hide__single').on('click', function (e) {
	                e.preventDefault();
	                var $target = $(this).siblings('.disclaimer__single');
	                swapText($target);
	                $(this).hide();
	                $(this).siblings('.disclaimer__show__single').show();
	            });
	            $('.disclaimer__accordian__title').on('click', function () {
	                $(this).parent().toggleClass('show');
	            });
	        };

	        if($disclaimer.length > 0) {
	            init();
	        }
		}
	});
</script>

		</style>
	
	
	
	
</div>
<div class="static-content aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
